League of Nations Political Committee Approves Russia's Admission to the League, to be Realized Today 25

General Assembly Delayed for Three Hours Yesterday

Formal Approval Expected

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly was originally scheduled to open at 3:30 p.m. today to welcome the first Soviet delegation. This meeting has now been postponed to 6:00 p.m. The Soviet delegation will be headed by Foreign Commissar Litvinov, with the Soviet Ambassador to Finland, Stein, Counselor of the Embassy in France, Rosenburg, and Legal Advisor to the Foreign Commissariat, Igoriapuv, as representatives to the General Assembly. In addition, there will be several experts. The delay in opening the General Assembly today seems to be because the head of the Soviet delegation, Litvinov, is still in Evian, France, drafting his speech with his staff, which is not yet completed. It also takes considerable time to complete the full powers procedures and contact the Moscow government. International observers believe that the issue of Soviet admission to the League of Nations has been thoroughly debated in the Sixth Committee, and there will be no further lengthy debate before its formal approval by the General Assembly today. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

A Debate in the Political Committee 26

The Small Country Group Vigorously Slandered Soviet Russia

The French Foreign Minister Gave a Persuasive Explanation

Vote – 38 Votes in Favor of Russian Membership

Result – 3 Countries Against, 7 Abstaining

(Geneva) The League of Nations Political Committee held a meeting today, and the audience was extremely crowded. After the meeting began, the small country group severely criticized Soviet Russia, but still decided to recommend to the General Assembly that Soviet Russia be accepted into the League of Nations. There were 38 countries in favor, 3 countries against, and 7 countries abstaining. It was found that this motion was a routine matter for the Political Committee, and no one expected any public attacks. It was not until the meeting was about to begin that they became aware of this.

Portuguese Representative Initiates Attack 27

Portuguese Foreign Minister da Matae was the first to slander the Soviet Russian government, saying that Soviet Russia's economic, political, and moral concepts are completely different from those of Portugal. If Soviet Russia joins the League of Nations, it will completely betray the principles of civilized countries. Therefore, although Portugal did not vote when Soviet Russia was voted as a permanent councilor on Saturday, it will vote against when the General Assembly votes to accept Soviet Russia into the League of Nations. (National News Agency dispatch on the 17th)

Switzerland Follows Up with Opposition 28

Swiss representative Motta followed, saying that Switzerland is the only country in the world that has joined the League of Nations through a referendum. Since the establishment of the League of Nations, Switzerland has advocated that the League of Nations should include all countries in the world. In 1920, he (Motta) gave a speech saying that he hoped that Soviet Russia could join, but the Swiss people have always opposed recognizing Soviet Russia. He believes that a government that practices communism and strives to spread communism is not compatible with the qualifications of a member of the League of Nations. The major powers have made expedient arguments on this matter, saying that after Soviet Russia joins the League of Nations and gets closer to other countries, its doctrines may change. The governments of Britain, France, and Italy have said to their friendly countries that the time for the Soviet Union to join the League has matured. These three countries certainly have this right. The mediation of the three countries for Soviet Russia to join the League is based on confidence and does not force other countries in any way. This is what we should say. However, Switzerland finds it difficult to agree with the views of these three countries. After Soviet Russia joins the League, various important issues will arise for debate in the Executive Council of the League of Nations, such as the issues of Georgia and Ukraine, which will not be eliminated due to the passage of time, and there are many people who advocate for them. Switzerland will also question Soviet Russia about anti-religious propaganda and ask it to explain.

Belgium Mentions Confiscation of Old Debts 29

Following Motta was Belgian Foreign Minister Jaspar, who said that Belgium has not yet restored diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia, the reason for which is the same as that stated by the Swiss representative. The reason is that Belgian people previously had 161 enterprises in Soviet Russia, worth hundreds of millions of gold francs, all of which were confiscated by Soviet Russia and none of which have been returned. However, Belgium will only abstain from voting on this Soviet Russian admission to the League of Nations and will not vote against it, so as not to hinder the efforts to maintain world peace and European order.

Argentina Claims No Diplomatic Relations with Russia 30

Next, Argentinian representative Cantilo spoke, Cantilo's words were simple, only stating that since the Argentinian embassy in Moscow was subjected to violent treatment, there have been no formal diplomatic relations between the two countries, so Argentina is abstaining from voting this time. Then, Dutch representative Viscount de Lovinfosse delivered a simple statement, saying that the Netherlands will vote against Soviet Russia's admission to the League of Nations, for the same reasons as those stated by Switzerland, Belgium, and Argentina.

French Foreign Minister Engages in a Verbal Battle with the Crowd 31

At this point, French Foreign Minister Barthou took the stage to present his views, saying that he takes the League of Nations Covenant as a guide, a witness, and a guarantee. Barthou then praised the words of Swiss representative Motta, saying that Motta had said that the mediation of Britain, France, and Italy for Soviet Russia to join the League was based entirely on confidence and did not force other countries in any way.

Off-site Negotiations are Not New 32

Barthou continued, saying that conducting talks off-site has become a traditional method in the League of Nations and is not a new beginning this time. In 1926, when Germany joined the League, the same procedure was adopted. At that time, the time spent in off-site talks was even longer than this time. The compromise for the Saar issue was also reached through off-site talks. Barthou also said that if Soviet Russia is admitted to the League, it is willing to abide by all the obligations stated in the League of Nations Covenant. This is the first time that Soviet Russia has said this. Barthou acknowledged that there has been a long period of disputes between Soviet Russia and the League of Nations in the past, but the League of Nations has always wanted to make its Covenant's first article a reality, as the founders wished the League of Nations to encompass the whole world, and the first article of the Covenant also clearly expresses this. Moreover, Swiss representative Motta also advocated Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations in 1920, but only with some reservations. The question today is whether the time for Soviet Russia to join the League has arrived.

French and Russian Debts Have Not Been Resolved 33

Barthou then replied to the points made by Motta and Jaspar criticizing Soviet Russia, saying that Switzerland and Belgium certainly each have their reasons for dissatisfaction, but does France not have them? For example, the debt issue between France and Russia has never been resolved. If what the two representatives said is true, then could France not also oppose Soviet Russia because of the debt issue?

Everything Should be Viewed from a Broader Perspective 34

But that is not what is being discussed today. We should view everything from a broader perspective, which is peace. The interests of the League of Nations are one with peace. Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations is beneficial to the League of Nations, and thus beneficial to peace. As for Soviet Russia's domestic politics, the Soviet system has changed since Lenin. This request for accession is clear evidence of this. We ask it for guarantees, and Soviet Russia does not treat us with vague words, which shows that Soviet Russian doctrines are changing. All of this does not mean that we want to interfere in Russia's internal affairs.

The Consequences of Shutting the Door are Serious 35

Barthou continued, (The League of Nations was originally established for the whole world, and now there is a country with a population of 180 million that is willing to join as a member in accordance with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant and does not set its own conditions. How can we regard this as a trivial matter and ignore it? This country asks to join a European international organization. Are you going to shut the door on it and let it suffer this insult, turning from bitterness to hatred of us? Where will rejecting Soviet Russia lead it? At this point, I do not wish to say any more.) At this point, Barthou said that the reason why some representatives oppose Soviet Russia is due to the incompatibility of doctrines. In fact, our recognition of Soviet Russia's accession to the League is a political necessity and there is no mysticism involved. The Portuguese representative said that isolation is the beginning of war. This is very true. Barthou also said, (If you reject Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations, then there will be serious events in the future that I do not wish to predict. Are you going to bear this responsibility?

World Peace Truly Depends On It 36

As I see it, Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations is beneficial to the League of Nations and to European peace, and even world peace. Think carefully about it. Motta said that history is the judge, but I say that posterity can also judge.) Barthou also stated that he supports the views of Britain and Italy and said that of the European countries, 22 have recognized Soviet Russia, and only five have not. If we consider the status of the 22 countries and their qualifications to represent Western civilization, then it is no exaggeration to say that all of Europe supports Soviet Russia. Barthou concluded by saying, (Precedent is not a reason. I have stated France's reasons. We dare to bear this responsibility to the world. Now that Soviet Russia wants to join hands with you, I hope you will not reject it from the international organization. If you vote in favor, then your enthusiasm and foresight for upholding world peace will be seen by the world.) (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

Britain and Italy Express Sincere Welcome 37

(Geneva) At the meeting of the Sixth Committee, the representatives of Switzerland, Belgium, Argentina, and the Netherlands, and French Foreign Minister Barthou spoke in succession. Then, British representative Lord Great Eden delivered a brief speech, saying that British foreign policy has always been based on the League of Nations, so it will spare no effort to support any action whose intention is to make the League of Nations have a (globally universal) nature. Italian representative Aloisi said that Italy was the first country to recognize the Soviet government. He, representing Italy, fully agreed with what Barthou and Eden said and also advocated that the Soviet Union join the League of Nations.

Czechoslovakia and Canada Echo Their Support 38

Czech representative Foreign Minister Beneš stated that the League of Nations should have a (globally universal) nature and that European peace also needs to be consolidated, but this is not possible without Soviet cooperation. He will therefore vote in favor of the Soviet Union's accession and firmly believes that not only European peace but also global peace truly depends on it. Canadian representative Skelton said that the Soviet Union and Canada have similar political principles and have several that are not adopted by other countries. He also acknowledged that the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations is a necessary measure to maintain world peace, so he decided to vote in favor.

Poland and Turkey Speak of Neighborly Relations 39

Polish representative Foreign Minister Beck said that Poland and the Soviet Union are neighboring countries and have a close relationship. They have signed many diplomatic documents proving the two countries' desire for peace.

Turkish representative Foreign Minister Rüştü said that Turkey has always hoped that the Soviet Union would join the League of Nations. The territories of Turkey and Russia are adjacent, and they have had friendly relations for fifteen years. During this period, the Soviet Union has continuously devoted itself to peace. For all these reasons, Turkey believes that the Soviet Union's accession is the most reliable factor for the League of Nations and world peace.

Chairman Concludes the Debate 40

After Rüştü finished speaking, no other country's representatives spoke in succession. Chairman Madariaga stood up and gave a speech, saying that after the Soviet Union joins, the (globally universal) nature of the League of Nations will be further advanced, which is truly gratifying.

Resolution Passed 41

Then a draft resolution was proposed and put to a vote. The text stated (The Sixth Committee, because the delegation of thirty countries sent an invitation to the Soviet Union on the fifteenth of this month, and the four countries of Denmark, Finland, Norway, and Sweden also sent letters to the Soviet Union, and because the Soviet Union has already responded, and in view of the Soviet Union's willingness to abide by the various obligations stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant, hereby recommends to the General Assembly that the Soviet Union be allowed to join the League of Nations). The chairman then used the roll-call method to conduct the vote. The three opposing countries were Portugal, the Netherlands, and Switzerland. The seven abstaining countries were Belgium, Luxembourg, Argentina, Venezuela, Paraguay, Nicaragua, and Cuba. The three absent countries were Uruguay, Finland, and Panama. The other thirty-eight countries all voted in favor. The League of Nations General Assembly is scheduled to meet on Tuesday afternoon, at which time Chairman Sandler will invite Madariaga to speak, followed by an invitation to the Soviet delegation to attend. It is expected that the Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov will deliver a speech to thank the chairman and the General Assembly. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

Russian Delegation Quietly Arrives in Geneva 42

Quietly Awaiting Assembly Vote

Preparing to Take the Stage

(Geneva) A Soviet Russian delegation of forty people suddenly arrived here at night. Most of the delegation members have been waiting in the upper Savoy area near Geneva for several days. The Russian delegation was guarded by a large police escort along the way. Upon reaching the shores of Lake Geneva, they all stayed in large apartments near the League of Nations Secretariat, quietly awaiting the official vote of the League of Nations General Assembly this afternoon before carrying out their duties as a member state of the League of Nations. (National Telegram, 18th)

Russia Could Assume Chairmanship at League of Nations Meeting Next Spring 43

Alphabetical Order Should Rotate to Russia

Saar Vote Causes Concern for Germany

(Geneva) According to observations from people here, when the League of Nations convenes its next session in January of next year, Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov is likely to be appointed as chairman. According to international custom, the chairmanship of each General Assembly is determined by the alphabetical order of the countries' names in French, and the representative of a certain country is nominated as chairman. As the current meeting is chaired by Czech Foreign Minister Beneš, the first letter of the Czech Republic's name in French is 'T', while the first letter of the Soviet Union's name in French is 'U'. Therefore, according to the order, the Soviet Russian representative is expected to be nominated as chairman for the next League of Nations meeting. However, the chairman has considerable influence over the proceedings of the meeting. Therefore, the Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations at this time means it must already be eyeing the chairman's position. Furthermore, when the League of Nations convenes its meeting next year, it will be at a critical juncture in resolving the Saar issue. Disputes after the Saar issue vote are also expected. Therefore, it would be a pity if the chairmanship were to fall into the hands of someone not deeply familiar with League of Nations affairs. (National Telegram, 17th)

(Berlin) After the Soviet Union joins the League of Nations, its Foreign Commissar Litvinov may serve as chairman when the League of Nations Administrative Council holds its meeting from January to May next year. German newspapers cannot help but be concerned about this matter, as the Saar issue is to be resolved in the spring of next year. The Evening Post stated that there is a more serious matter, namely that the Socialist Party of the Swiss canton of Geneva may unite with its Communist Party to form a united front. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

Russian Newspaper's Triumphant Remarks 44

From Enemies to Friends in Peace and Cooperation

Japanese and German Ambitions Can Cease

(Moscow) The Pravda newspaper published an editorial exclusively on the Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations, stating: (Currently, there are some countries attempting to re-divide the world, and they first plan to sacrifice the Soviet Union to expand themselves, proposing plans for an anti-Soviet war and seeking help from the entire imperialist world. However, an anti-Soviet war will inevitably lead to the outbreak of contradictions among all imperialists and could become the turning point for a global war. Therefore, although some capitalist countries are hostile to the Soviet Union, they ultimately harbor a fear that the anti-Soviet actions of imperialist adventurers could be the prelude to a new world war, a war that would target several imperialist countries. (Since Germany and Japan withdrew from the League, most of the major and minor powers in the League have deemed the policy of leaning towards war as formidable. However, they have failed to restrain Japan's aggressive policies or prevent Germany's expansion of armaments. As the war crisis becomes increasingly serious, they are seeking new forces whose capabilities are sufficient to resist the war crisis. These forces are willing to participate in the creation and safeguarding of peace and can be responsible for this defense work. Although they are hostile to socialism, they cannot help but turn their attention to the Soviet Union, as the Soviet Union has proven its steadfastness and decisiveness in its struggle to maintain peace.) Under the current circumstances, the Soviet Union has never refused any form of cooperation in the capitalist world that is concerned with preventing war. Stalin has clearly defined the Soviet Union's attitude towards the League of Nations. This attitude is determined by (1) the attitude of the League of Nations member states towards the Soviet Union, (2) their attitude towards aggressive plans (regardless of where they come from), and (3) the League of Nations' ability to prevent war (as Stalin mentioned). This is absolutely clear. The Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations means that a great power has joined as a powerful force striving for peace and as the greatest force in the international arena. When joining, it deeply wishes to utilize all possibilities to prevent war (even the smallest should be utilized). (TASS News Agency, 17th)

Russia and Albania Restore Diplomatic Relations 45

Rome: The Soviet Union and Albania have restored normal diplomatic relations from today. Regarding this matter, notes were exchanged between Soviet Chargé d'Affaires Gelfand and Albanian Chargé d'Affaires Rodre at the Soviet Embassy. (Havas News Agency, 17th)

Austrian Prime Minister Returns to Vienna 46

Will Not Make a Trip to Paris

Vienna: After returning from Geneva, Prime Minister Schuschnigg issued a statement reporting on the results of his trip to Geneva. Although he did not mention which European capital he would visit at an appropriate time, well-informed sources believe that Schuschnigg will most likely make a trip to Paris. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

Italian Youth Receive Military Training 47

Rome: The government has issued two orders stipulating that from now on, all Italian people must undergo two years of military training from the age of eight until the age of ten. After the age of ten, they will be incorporated into the Fascist Youth Organization and receive youth military education until the age of eighteen. After the age of eighteen, they will be formed into the Youth Party Army, which will be responsible for their training by the Fascist Party Army. The Youth Party Army must drill every Sunday. Employers who prevent employees from drilling will be fined. The government has established a special agency to coordinate the liaison between the regular army and military training institutions. Furthermore, military education courses must be added to all Italian middle schools and universities. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

US Senate Investigates Aircraft Industry 48

Claims Germany is Determined to Form an Air Force

(Washington) During the US Senate Committee's investigation into the arms trade today, Hamilton, the European representative of the United Aircraft Export Corporation, testified that he reported to the company in 1933 that Germany was determined to organize an air force and this concern is gradually taking concrete form. He also stated that this year, the company sold 176 aircraft engines and eight aircraft to Germany. Based on his conversations with various German departments, the Germans' attention extends far beyond transportation matters. The number of transactions completed in 1932 was 234,000 yuan, which increased to 1,445,000 yuan in 1933. (Reuters News Agency, 17th)

League of Nations Yearbook of Military Trade 49

Published in Geneva

(Geneva) The League of Nations Yearbook of Military Trade was published today, stating that from 1932 onwards, countries neighboring Germany actively increased their armaments. The total amount of arms purchased from other countries by Belgium, Poland, Switzerland, and the Netherlands in 1932 reached more than US$2.7 million. (National News Agency, 18th)

German Circles Host Banquet for Chinese Inspection Group 50

(Berlin) The German Industrial Association, the China Problem Research Association, and the Far East Association jointly hosted a banquet yesterday for the Chinese government's military transportation inspection group led by Chinese Vice Minister of Transportation Yu Feipeng and 17th Army Commander Xu Tingyao. Chinese Ambassador to Germany Liu Chongjie, embassy staff, and important figures in the German economic community, such as German Railway Company President Dr. Dorpmüller, Central Bank Vice President Dr. Devas, and Count Grotze, were also invited to attend. The chairman of the China Problem Research Association, Leitzmann, delivered a welcoming speech. Chinese Ambassador to Germany Liu Chongjie gave a reply on behalf of the inspection group members, stating that the dredger manufactured in Germany for China was recently launched, which is a clear demonstration of international cooperation for peace. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

Eastern European Pact Negotiations to Continue Despite German Opposition 51

New Developments Expected After Russia Joins the League of Nations

(Berlin) It was heard here today that the German government is now opposing any pact initiated in Paris guaranteeing peace in Eastern Europe. Germany is now discussing announcing that it is willing to accept a kind of pact that must include collective non-aggression obligations and consultations between the countries concerned in times of political crisis. It is said that Germany's refusal to sign the Eastern Locarno Pact is due to fears that Russian and French troops may one day revisit its borders. At the same time, according to a Reuters dispatch from Geneva, League of Nations officials now believe that with Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations, negotiations on the conclusion of the Eastern Locarno Pact will resume, disregarding German opposition. (Reuters News Agency, 18th)

Page 8

Hirota Sends Yoshida as Special Envoy to Russia and Various European and American Countries to Address Next Year's International Crisis 52

(Tokyo) In order to address the international crisis of 1935 and 1936, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will accurately convey the true situation of Japan's advancement to foreign envoys. At the same time, it will seek smooth contact with the trends of domestic public opinion to avoid delaying opportunities. Therefore, the selection of envoys to be sent abroad is extremely prudent. As a result of discussions at the leadership meeting on the 18th, it was decided to send Mr. Shigeru Yoshida, former Ambassador to Italy, as a representative of the Foreign Minister. The ambassador has agreed. One or two section chief-level officials will be selected from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as attendants. They are scheduled to depart from Tokyo in early October. The trip will last approximately four months, passing through Northwest Siberia to the Soviet Union, Poland, Germany, Belgium, France, and the United Kingdom. Then, they will cross from the UK to the United States. All Japanese embassies visited along the way must be inspected, and Japan's appropriate and unwavering ultimate policy must be conveyed in order to break through the international crisis and practically supervise the envoys stationed abroad so that they can follow it. This is the most critical recent development, and the general public is focusing its attention on it. (Japan Union Telegraph, 18th)

Direct Telephone Call Between Japan and Germany 53

Hamburg, Germany: A direct telephone call between Hamburg, Germany, and Tokyo, Japan, was tested for the first time today. The results were very satisfactory. The Hamburg American Shipping Company spoke directly with its representative in Tokyo, and the sound was clearly audible. (Havas News Agency, 18th)

American Journalist Group Visits Japan to Investigate Japan-Manchuria Relations 54

Yokohama: The leader of the American journalist group visiting Japan this time is Mr. Wilbur Forrest, editor of the Washington Post. According to his statement on behalf of the group: "We represent the American press and will frankly introduce Japan and Manchuria to the United States based on what we have seen and heard. This is what we expect. We also intend to exchange comments on Japan's circles, and we must deepen our proper understanding of Japan-Manchuria relations. In the future, the relationship between Japan and the United States may take this as an opportunity to become closer, which would be fortunate." (Japan United Press, 18th)

Japanese Combined Fleet Arrives in Dalian 55

(Dalian) More than sixty warships belonging to the Combined Fleet arrived in Dalian at 10:30 a.m. on the 18th. Commander-in-Chief Admiral Suetsugu and Imperial Prince Captain Takamatsu landed at 2:30 p.m. to meet representatives from all walks of life. (Japan Union Telegraph, 18th)

New Siamese Cabinet 56

Bangkok: Siamese Prime Minister Phahon submitted his cabinet's resignation on Friday. Today, King Prajadhipok ordered Phahon to continue serving as Prime Minister and form a new cabinet. (Reuters News Agency, 17th)

Dutch Parliament Opens 57

Queen Delivers New Address

Communist Members Forced Out of Meeting

The Hague: The Dutch Parliament opened today. The Queen attended the meeting and delivered an address, emphasizing the need to maintain a sound national financial position. She stated that increasing taxes is impossible, so it is necessary to reduce expenditures, especially focusing on expanding the domestic market. The government wants to prevent the trend of increasing security forces, but it must also consider this trend in its national defense plans. The Queen's address was disrupted by Communist members of parliament, who rose up and caused disturbances. However, the authorities had prepared for this and detectives escorted them out of the chamber. The Queen then left the chamber with her daughter and returned to the palace by car. The crowd outside the chamber cheered to show their respect. (Reuters News Agency, 18th)

Serious Labor Unrest in the United States 58

(New York) The textile workers' strike in the United States has entered its third week today, but the situation is even darker than before. Strike Committee Chairman Gorman has issued a desperate appeal stating that if the strike is not resolved within this week, all non-striking parts of the textile industry will also shut down. If this threat is realized, 100,000 workers in the dyeing industry, rayon industry, underwear industry, knitting industry, and carpet industry will be affected. Several clashes between strikers and the National Guard occurred today, but there were no major casualties. A team of National Guardsmen in Berman was ordered to maintain order at a knitting factory. A thousand picketers shouted at them, "You are creating a revolution!" But the National Guard calmly advanced and pointed their bayonets at them. The picketers quickly retreated. In Water Village, Maine, picketers planned to attack a factory, and bricks flew, shattering many windows. In Newman, Georgia, many picketers were arrested by the National Guard. The Governor of Georgia, in view of the seriousness of the labor unrest, has declared martial law in areas where disturbances are difficult for local officials to handle. A detention center is being prepared for construction in Atlanta, protected by barbed wire, to detain the arrested strikers. Thirty-eight teams of the National Guard have been dispatched in North Carolina, and twenty-four teams have also been dispatched in South Carolina. Two hundred and nine cotton mills have closed in North Carolina, and two hundred and eighty-two are operating. Ninety mills have closed in South Carolina, and ninety-nine are operating. (Reuters News Agency, 17th)

Major Fire in Alaska 59

Entire Town of Nome Destroyed

(Washington) News was received here today from Nome, Alaska, stating that all government offices and the entire commercial district of Nome were destroyed by a major fire. A US warship stationed on the west coast of Alaska has sailed to Nome to provide relief to 400 victims.

A subsequent telegram from Nome stated that the entire town was destroyed by fire. The wind fanned the flames, causing them to spread. Currently, only one hotel, one government office, and a few residential houses remain standing. Two Eskimos attempted to retrieve their belongings but were unable to escape and perished in the flames. Fortunately, there were no other deaths. Several people were injured while using explosives to create firebreaks. Nome is a coal-producing area. In 1900, it had a population of 12,000. Since then, the population has gradually decreased. According to a survey in 1930, the population had decreased to 1,200. (Japan Union Telegraph, 18th)

Huang Musong Telegraphed Nanjing Regarding Commemoration and Enthronement Ceremony Date 60

(Nanjing) Huang Musong recently telegraphed Nanjing from Tibet, reporting that after arriving in Lhasa, he had visited major temples to pay his respects and the ceremony is now complete. The date for the commemoration and enthronement ceremony will be selected on an auspicious day. It is also said that Huang will return to Nanjing next month. (Central News Agency, 18th)

Lu Jiang County Magistrate Punished for Corruption 61

(Nanjing) Supervisory Committee member Liu Eqing impeached Zhang Liying, former magistrate of Lu Jiang County, Anhui, Gao Zipei, the current magistrate, and Zhang Jinghan, the former trial officer, for dereliction of duty and corruption. The Central Disciplinary Committee decided to demote Zhang Liying by two grades and re-promote him, issued a written reprimand to Gao Zipei, and dismissed Zhang Jinghan from office and suspended him from employment for three years. (Central News Agency, 18th)

Judges Who Passed the Higher Civil Service Examination Sent to Training Institute for Training 62

(Nanjing) Thirty-two people who passed the first Higher Civil Service Examination for judges were sent by the Ministry of Justice to study in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces for a period of one year. Now that the term has expired, the Ministry has specifically transferred them back to the Judicial Training Institute for training, which will begin in November and last for one year, after which their qualifications will be confirmed. Huai Bei Salt Merchants from Bengbu Petition 63

(Nanjing) More than twenty people, including Bengbu Huai Bei salt merchants Chang Jiichang, came to Nanjing on the 18th to petition the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, stating that during the winter of the previous year, Transport Commissioner Miao Qiujie, due to insufficient tax revenue at the Public Enterprise Office, discussed with the Bengbu salt merchants to collect pre-tax payments, borrowing a total of approximately 3 million yuan. However, Transport Commissioner Miao has repeatedly forgotten the previous agreement to clear the debts within a specified period, otherwise new taxes will be levied, causing the merchants to suffer losses. They requested that the Central Government order Miao to maintain the original agreement to rescue the salt merchants. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

It requested that the collection be stopped. Various Yuan, Departments, and Commissions Discuss Compiling Political Work Reports 66

(Nanjing) With the Fifth Plenary Session of the KMT Central Executive Committee approaching, at 2 p.m. on the 18th, the government convened those in charge of compiling political work reports from various Yuan, departments, and commissions at the First Conference Hall to discuss the format and content of the political work reports. Ministry of Communications Plans to Open Sichuan-Guizhou Air Route 67

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications plans to open an air route from Chongqing via Guiyang to Kunming. However, as this route is not within the scope of the China National Aviation Corporation, the Ministry of Communications has decided to operate it itself, entrusting the company to handle it. The required start-up costs are budgeted at 250,000 yuan and have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. Once the funds are raised, the aircraft will be purchased. The locations of the airports along the route have been telegraphed by the Ministry of Communications to the authorities in Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan provinces to find locations and report back. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Commander of the US Far East Fleet Leaves Peiping for Qinhuangdao 73

Manager of the Oriental Travel Agency Goes to Peiping 74

(Beiping) Since the Oriental Travel Agency took over the Peiping-Shenyang train service, both passenger and freight traffic have been underdeveloped, and it has been losing money for the past month. The company is afraid that it cannot withstand long-term losses, so it has proposed reorganization, but it has not yet been approved by the authorities. The company's manager, Zhang Shuiqi, came to Peiping this morning to meet with Yin Tong, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, to discuss rescue measures. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Northeast Righteous Army Bravely Fights the Enemy During the Second Anniversary of the National Crisis 95

Derailment of the East China Railway Train Inflicts Heavy Losses on the Enemy

Righteous Army Attacks Japanese Forestry Company

Over One Hundred Wounded Japanese Soldiers Transported Back to Japan

Harbin Correspondence: The Righteous Armies in various parts of the Northeast, during this time of national crisis, are increasingly brave in resisting the enemy and saving the country. The details are as follows: On the 3rd of this month, the 303rd Russian freight train, dispatched from Bogula on the eastern section of the China Eastern Railway, was traveling between Xiaojiu Station and Mifeng Station when the railway was sabotaged in advance by the Righteous Army. When the train arrived at this location, the locomotive and four freight cars were overturned and derailed. The Righteous Army, ambushing on both sides, fired all at once. Many crew members, police, and Japanese railway guard troops were killed or wounded. Rescue trains were dispatched from Harbin and other places to rush to the scene to rescue. However, the rescue train departing from Harbin was delayed, and by the time it arrived, the Righteous Army had safely seized what they could and left. Also, at Henglizi, 12 kilometers south of Pingan Station on the Rabin Line, more than 400 Righteous Army members nicknamed "Delin" suddenly appeared. Upon receiving the report, the Japanese and puppet forces immediately dispatched the Taniguchi unit of the Japanese army from Wuchang County to rush to the battle. On the night of the 5th, the Righteous Army broke through the encirclement. As a result, Japanese soldiers Kondo, Inaba, and Umezaki were killed in battle. In addition, Ito was also seriously injured. Also, at 6:00 AM on the 8th of this month, the railway construction site in the forest area of the Japanese Kondo Forestry Company in Yabulini on the eastern section of the China Eastern Railway was suddenly attacked by about 40 Righteous Army members. Nakamura Heizaburo, the manager of the forest area, was seriously injured. Three people, including the branch chief, the self-defense corps leader, and the telegrapher, were killed. Also, at 7:00 AM on the same day, a large number of Righteous Army members suddenly appeared 40 kilometers away at the junction of Gaoling and Liudaogouzi. The 91st train was also overturned. Also, four long-distance buses departing from Tonghe on the eastern border of Liaoning and heading to Shanchenzhen had just arrived at Erlidi, southeast of Sanjianbao, when they were suddenly attacked by more than 60 Righteous Army members. Twelve Japanese soldiers were killed or wounded, with three dead. Matsuno, Inoue, and another Japanese merchant were killed. Nine people were injured (Morimura Jinzo, the governor, and eight others). Two Japanese merchants, Yoshimi, and two Manchurians were captured. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese and puppet forces urgently dispatched teams from Shanchenzhen, Tonghua, and Liuhe to rush to support. After fierce fighting, both sides suffered casualties again.

Dalian Correspondence: Recently, after the Righteous Army rose up to resist Japan in northern Manchuria, the Japanese army suffered repeated heavy losses. The number of deaths and injuries is heard of every day. Recently, another 103 wounded soldiers, under the care of 11 nurses including Nursing Officer Yamashita, arrived in Dalian at 6:20 AM on the 7th of this month. Many Japanese officials and civilians came to welcome them. They were admitted to the Ojima-cho Garrison Hospital and are scheduled to return to Japan proper by ship around the 10th. Also, a group of educational inspectors from Ehime Prefecture, Japan, after completing their inspection of the entire Manchuria, were returning south from Harbin when their train was also overturned and attacked by the Righteous Army. Among the 29 members of the group, five died and four were seriously injured. The remaining 20 members arrived in Dalian at 3:00 PM on the 7th, along with the injured, and were comforted by the Japanese Women's Association and other Japanese people in the VIP room of the station, and will soon return home by boat. (Northeast News Agency)

Court Record of Hotel Owner Raping Young Girl 96

(Songjiang) Yuan Quanlin, the owner of the Far East Hotel on Xidajie in this city, raped Shun Di, the 15-year-old adopted daughter of Mrs. Wang Zhou, the owner of the Zhenxin Hotel, on June 28, and stole her jewelry box and fled. Mrs. Wang Zhou filed a lawsuit in court. Yuan, upon hearing the news, disappeared. Although his family searched for him, there was no trace of him. The case was heard in court today. The defendant was absent. The plaintiff, Mrs. Wang Zhou, brought her adopted daughter to court to testify about the rape. She said that Yuan Quanlin took advantage of Wang's absence to sneak into her house and began to harass her adopted daughter, then forcibly raped her. The adopted daughter's screams were heard by the tea boy Wang Zizhai, Zhang Honghai, and the police officer Wu Guanyuan, who was on guard at the Maluqiao station. Officer Wu shined his flashlight on her without error. Gu Changqi, who was cooling off, also heard the screams, which can be used as evidence. After the rape, he threw the soiled pants into the Houhe, and before leaving, he stole a jewelry box and fled. The investigating official instructed that the raped Shun Di be sent to Songjiang Hospital for examination. The defendant's wife also hired lawyers Ni Bingshi and Zheng Wen to write a defense, and also filed a counterclaim, stating that Yuan and Wang Zhou were uncle and aunt. They once lived together, and then suddenly separated and each held evidence. Recently, because Yuan opened the Songhui Hotel, which conflicted with Wang Zhou's Zhenjin Hotel, they began to slander each other. Now that Yuan has fled, she is filing a counterclaim, etc. Both sides hold their own views, and it is unknown how to resolve the case.

Implementing Forced Registration of Smokers 102

The County Anti-Smoking Committee has made up its mind to implement smoking bans. Committee Chairman Yan Shenyu stated that the deadline for smoker registration in urban and rural areas is approaching, but many smokers in various districts are still waiting and watching, which violates the government's original intention of banning smoking within a specified time. Yesterday, he specially formulated a simple method of forced registration, scheduled to implement forced registration, and instructed the County Public Security Bureau and the public security sub-bureaus and district public offices to implement it. At the same time, he ordered Wang Ji, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and the sub-bureau chiefs and patrol officers of the direct subordinate branch offices, to concurrently serve as members of the investigation and seizure group of the County Anti-Smoking Association. The forced registration method is as follows: 1. From September 21st to the 30th in urban areas, and from September 26th to the 30th in rural areas, all unregistered smokers must undergo forced registration. 2. All investigation teams and registration points are responsible for forcing smokers to fulfill the registration requirements. They will be assessed based on whether the investigation of smokers in their respective jurisdictions is thorough, in order to determine rewards and punishments. 3. If any investigation team or registration point finds any smokers who have not yet registered, they shall immediately summon them to the registration point and order them to register, and collect the fee. If they resist the summons, they may change the summons to detention. 4. If an unregistered smoker refuses to register after being summoned to the registration point, they may be escorted to the County Anti-Smoking Association for review. 5. If an unregistered smoker declares that they have quit smoking, they must fill out a separate quit-smoking application form and submit it to the association for record. Otherwise, they must obtain a license and must not attempt to confuse or evade the regulations. 6. When enforcing forced registration of smokers, in addition to the license fee that the smoker should pay, the investigation teams and the enforcing police officers at the registration points must not extort additional fees. Violators will be severely punished.

The Notorious Bandit Was Identified by the Victim Without Error 103

(Changzhou) The case of the robbery at the home of Zhao Songping, a gentry in Qingguo Lane in Wuyi City, on January 8th of last year, in which the gatekeeper He Canhai was shot and killed, caused a sensation at the time. Recently, one of the main perpetrators of the case, Yu Congchang, was captured, and the original stolen soft satin mandarin jacket and table carpet were recovered. The sub-perpetrators were interrogated repeatedly, but they all denied committing the robbery. They said that after the robbery occurred, they were once captured by the investigation team and handed over to Mr. Zhao for identification. Mr. Zhao was unable to identify them at the time, so why do you now say that I did it? The reason is that this bandit is the brother of Mr. Zhao's coachman, and he once served as a soldier. When he committed the robbery, he spoke with a Haiqiang accent and wore makeup and a beard. At the time of identification, he had a white beard and face, and spoke with a local accent. At that time, Mr. Zhao suspected him but did not dare to identify him. Magistrate Hou urged Mr. Zhao to go to the county to identify him, as the perpetrator firmly refused to confess. Zhao replied to Hou that he would wait until the perpetrator grew his beard in prison before identifying him. The perpetrator has been in prison for many days, and his beard has grown. Magistrate Hou immediately sent Secretary Yang to interrogate him on the afternoon of the 17th, and also notified Mr. Zhao to come to court. The perpetrator was given a press-haired呢帽(woolen hat) by the bailiffs, and wore a green cloth shirt (the clothes he was wearing when he committed the robbery). His beard was also long. When Mr. Zhao arrived in court, he saw that the perpetrator's appearance and dress were exactly the same as when he committed the robbery. He immediately told the court that it was indeed the perpetrator who committed the robbery, and there was no error. After another round of questioning, the perpetrator was ordered to fingerprint and dismissed from court.

Young Man Poses as Western Doctor to Swindle 104

(Jiangyin) Recently, a young man posing as a Western doctor has been going to wealthy families in the city to carry out scams. A few days ago, a young man in Western clothing suddenly came to the home of Mr. Sha in Qingguo Lane, claiming to be the director of a certain hospital in Wuxi and said that he received a quick letter from his home and came to treat his illness. After being entertained by the female servant, he learned that he wasn't home, so his wife came out. At that time, there were several maids watching. The young man pointed to one of the maids and said that she had a disease and would soon be in danger, so he would treat her free of charge. He took out a silver needle, poked it into her back, then used a magnetic cup, baked it with a match, closed the silver needle, and took it out after a while. As expected, there was a cup of phlegm. The wife believed that he was a famous doctor, because after passing through the door, she often grieved about having no children, so she was eager to have a son and asked the young man to treat her. The young man also used the previous method to extract three cups of cold phlegm first, and then said that prescribing and decocting medicine would be troublesome, so he would give the family nine pills specially made by the Zhang mansion in Wuxi, each pill costing seven yuan. Sha's wife agreed and immediately paid 63 yuan. The young man got the money and made an excuse that he had to go to another family to treat their illness and went back to Wuxi, and then went out without knowing where he went. When he returned home, he learned that he had been scammed, and said that the phlegm in the cup was a chemical reaction. The Medical Association learned about this and, believing that it damaged the reputation of Western medicine, sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau urging them to arrest him to prevent people from being deceived.

Autumn Rain Hinders Cotton Harvest 105

(Nantong) The cotton fields in various counties under Nantong and the coastal reclamation areas of Huainan are now in the peak season for cotton picking, but the continuous autumn rain has caused many of the cotton bolls to rot due to rain immersion. The area suffered from drought at the beginning of this year, followed by autumn overcast weather. The losses to cotton farmers are extremely severe. It is estimated that the value of cotton production in the Jianghua area this year is about 56 million yuan, of which 9 million yuan belongs to the reclamation area.

Zhuyi Bandit in the Four Counties of Xin, Sheng, Fenghua Surrenders 106

(Hangzhou) Sun Lichao, a bandit in Fenghua, Sheng County, Xin Chang and Fenghua and Ninghai counties, whose nickname is Sun Laoer, from Sunjiatian, Xinchang County. His brother, Libiao, was also a bandit. He was captured by the Provincial Government in Shanghai in the 20th year of the Republic of China. He died by suicide by taking poison on the way to Hangzhou. Libiao's subordinates were scattered in the four counties, and then elected Lichao as their leader. The police force gradually increased. Recently, he regretted being a bandit and surrendered to the Standing Army of the county. The captain of the team telegraphed the Second Security Branch for instructions. He was instructed to escort Sun to discuss surrender matters.

Suicide Due to Economic Hardship 107

Shen Changfa, a native of Shaoxing, who was originally a weaver, lived on Dadongmen Straight Street in Xiashao. In recent years, due to the failure of the silk industry, he switched to selling small commodities for a living. He also lost all his capital. He then made a living by pulling a rickshaw, using his income to support his family. Recently, his old mother was critically ill. The family had pawned everything and owed a lot of rent, so they could not afford medical treatment. Shen developed a world-weary mentality, went to Huanglong Cave in West Lake and hanged himself. He was later discovered and resuscitated with artificial respiration and sent to the police station for investigation.

Opening of the Agricultural Bank Embezzlement Case 108

(Jiaxing) The Jiaxing County Farmers Bank previously experienced a major theft, losing over 40,000 yuan in cash and banknotes. A package of gold jewelry was also deposited by a Mr. Tu. Subsequently, a special investigator from the provincial government was dispatched to Jiaxing to investigate the bank. Discrepancies in the accounts' income and expenditure were discovered. The bank's chief cashier, Xu Fukang, and related staff member, Tu Yiran, were immediately investigated. Manager Wu Heshu, fearing punishment, fled. The county government then transferred the two bank employees, Xu and Tu, along with laborers Tu Haigen, Song Shiyuan, and suspects Zhi Asi, Feng Xingsun, Chen Afa, and others, a total of nine people, to the court for interrogation. After the investigation was concluded, they were collectively prosecuted for embezzlement. Judge Zhou Wending of the criminal court opened the trial on the morning of the 18th. Xu and Tu hired lawyer Jiang Weixian to defend them. After a detailed interrogation regarding the falsification of accounts and the circumstances of the theft, bank personnel claimed that the forgery of accounts was instructed by the manager, and they had no knowledge of the theft. Chen Afa and others claimed they had no involvement whatsoever. The court ordered Tu Yiran, Xu Fukang, Song Shiyuan, and Tu Haigen to each provide a cash bail of 1,000 yuan. Chen Afa and the other seven were ordered to each provide a written bail of 1,000 yuan. Tu and others requested to change to written bail in court, which was denied. Since they had no cash, they were immediately returned to custody.

Local News 109

(September 18th) National Humiliation Commemorated This Week

All Sectors Hold Commemoration Rally 110

Citywide Suspension of Entertainment and Half-Mast Flag in Mourning

Over Three Thousand Members of Youth Propaganda Corps

Tao Baichuan Reports on Road and Maritime Party Department Conference

According to the Central News Agency, yesterday was the third anniversary of the September 18th National Humiliation Incident. All government agencies, organizations, and schools in the city flew flags at half-mast to express mourning. At 11:00 AM, all citizens stopped working for five minutes, stood up to commemorate and vow to avenge the national humiliation, and expressed condolences to the fallen soldiers and martyred compatriots who resisted Japan. All amusement venues in the city were closed. Restaurants and taverns also suspended banquets. The military and police authorities, fearing that reactionary elements might take the opportunity to cause trouble, took extra precautions. The city's Party headquarters also convened a commemoration rally at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps at 10:00 AM, gathering representatives from all sectors. Representatives from all sectors gave mournful speeches. The details are as follows:

(Venue Decoration) A bamboo cloth banner was hung above the entrance of the assembly, reading "Shanghai All Sectors Representatives September 18th Third Anniversary Commemoration Rally." The venue was plastered with various stimulating slogans. Ten slogans were hung on the stage, along with a portrait of the late Founding Father and the Party and national flag. The Municipal Public Security Bureau military band also participated in playing mournful music. Tao Baichuan, Mayor Wu (represented by Chen Kecheng), Jiang Huaisu, Zhu Xuefan, Yu Zhenhui, and Yu Zuoting, all members of the Presidium, arrived on time. The atmosphere at the venue was solemn.

(Rally Order) (1) Music, (2) Sing the Party Anthem, (3) Pay the Highest Respects to the Party and National Flag and the Late Founding Father's Portrait, (4) The Chairman Respectfully Reads the Late Founding Father's Last Will, (5) Observe Three Minutes of Silence to Mourn the Compatriots Who Died in the Northeast, (6) Report, (7) Speeches.

(Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

(Chairman's Report) After the formalities were completed, Tao Baichuan, as the Chairman of the meeting, gave a report, stating: "Three years have passed since the September 18th Incident. During these three years, over four million square miles of our Northeast territory have continued to be occupied by the violent Japanese, and over thirty million people have continued to be trampled upon by the violent Japanese. Tracing back to the violent Japanese invasion of Ryukyu and then the invasion of the Northeast, and now eyeing North China, they have become the greatest enemy of our Chinese nation. Their ambition is to rule our entire China. Therefore, if our nation wants to survive, we must overthrow Japanese imperialism in order to avenge this extraordinary humiliation. When we are unwilling to submit temporarily, we should unite as one, strengthen our national power, consolidate our national defense, and especially pay attention to the following four things: First, strengthen military equipment. In terms of the air force, we should have two to three thousand airplanes. In terms of the navy, we should prepare for hundreds of thousands of tons of naval vessels. In terms of the army, the entire nation should be able to go to the battlefield and fight the enemy with their lives. Second, strive for political integrity and make all officials in the country serve the country with a spirit of sacrifice. As Yue Wumu said, (Scholars do not love money, and soldiers are not afraid of death). Only in this way can we reverse this crisis. In particular, the central government should have sufficient power to command the entire country, and all local governments should obey the central government. Then China can achieve true unity, and the national situation can turn from danger to safety and from weakness to strength. Third, promote economic construction, such as all transportation tools and industries, which should be actively promoted so that huge amounts of leakage are no longer lost overseas every year. Fourth, reform education. Education is the foundation of a nation. Our revenge cannot be effective in one day or one night. Therefore, we should use education to cultivate healthy citizens. Then, even if we cannot immediately avenge this great hatred, our children and grandchildren will be able to continue this ambition and avenge this extraordinary humiliation." Finally, regarding the treatment of symptoms, we must achieve national unity politically, and socially, all people should earnestly boycott Japanese goods and resist for a long time. We should never forget the matter of revenge, and then victory can be predicted. Then, Mayor Wu representing Chen Kecheng, Zhu Xuefan, and Jiang Huaisu delivered speeches. Reflections of Gu Weijun and Wang Zhengting on China's Failure to Be Elected as a Non-Permanent Member of the League of Nations Council 111

Unfortunately Not Elected This Year, Can Still Compete Next Year

Citizens Should Focus on Internal Affairs, Then There Will Be Foreign Affairs

According to the Central News Agency, China's request to obtain the right to be re-elected as a non-permanent member of the Council of the League of Nations was rejected by the League of Nations General Assembly on the 17th, and Turkey succeeded as a non-permanent member. China's failure to be elected this time will lead to a lack of good contributions to the League of Nations on the Far East issue, which is of great importance to the future of the League of Nations. The Central News Agency reporter immediately inquired about China's failure to be elected with Gu Weijun, China's Minister to France, and Wang Zhengting, the former Minister of Foreign Affairs, who are now in Shanghai. Their talks were as follows:

(China Can Compete Again Next Year) According to Gu, there are five permanent members of the Council of the League of Nations and nine non-permanent members. Last year, one seat was added, totaling ten seats, for a total of fifteen seats. Those elected are all from countries in Europe and the Americas. In the first session of the League of Nations Council, no representative from an Asian country was elected. At that time, I was appointed to attend the General Assembly, so I suggested two principles to the General Assembly: (1) Non-permanent members should pay attention to regional distribution, (2) Countries that have not been elected as permanent or non-permanent members should be elected in rotation. This was well received by various countries, so at the 1920 General Assembly, based on this principle, China obtained the votes of the majority of member states and was elected as a non-permanent member representing Asian countries. This time, when the term expired and the election was held, China's request for re-election failed to obtain the two-thirds majority of the General Assembly, resulting in rejection, and the General Assembly elected Turkey to succeed. But next year, China can still participate in the election again. As for the number of seats for representatives of Asian countries as non-permanent members, it does not seem necessary to increase them, because in previous General Assemblies, those who proposed to increase the number of seats for non-permanent members were severely attacked by the representatives of the majority of member states, because there are not many Asian countries, and there is no need to increase the number of seats.

(League of Nations Lacking) Minister Gu believes that China's request for re-election as a non-permanent member was rejected by the General Assembly, which is a great pity, not only for China, but also for the League of Nations itself, because China is a country that loves peace and supports the League of Nations most strongly, and it is indeed necessary for it to be re-elected. In other words, if China is re-elected, it will also benefit the League of Nations itself. Gu also said that China is a country that has been invaded by force, and the fact that it has been invaded by force has been proven by the League of Nations and has a resolution. For the sake of respecting the League of Nations Covenant, China's request for re-election was denied, which is a great regret. At this time of tension in the Far East situation, special attention should be paid to peace in the international community. Now that China cannot be re-elected, the League of Nations will inevitably lack a considerable contribution to the Far East issue, which is a pity for the future of the League of Nations.

(Turkey Has Been Planning to Compete for a Long Time) As for why China failed to be elected this time, it is because Turkey joined the League of Nations not long ago. After the European War, Turkey worked hard to revitalize and became a new country. It is very active in international activities, such as sending ambassadors to various countries. Turkey is located between Europe and Asia, so it is called a European country in Europe and an Asian country in Asia. This time, it actually won a seat as a non-permanent member in the name of an Asian country. Turkey's plan to win this seat is not a matter of a day or two. Last year, it tried to take on the positions of Chairman of the Council of the League of Nations and non-permanent members, but all failed. This time, it came back with great ambition. Turkey's foreign policy has always been in the same direction as France, Russia, and the Little Entente. Persia also participated in the non-permanent member election before, but then announced that it would give way to Turkey. From this, we can see the strength of Turkey's activities in the international community. Since Turkey is a newly joined member of the League of Nations and has not been elected to any position in the League of Nations, it is no coincidence that it achieved better results in this election.

(Soviet Union's Joining the League Has Nothing to Do With Us) As for the Soviet Union's imminent joining of the League of Nations, while China happened to fail in the election at this time, Minister Gu believes that there is no direct relationship.

(Never Forget Recovering Lost Territory) Yesterday was the September 18th Memorial Day. When Minister Gu met with reporters, he also expressed his feelings, saying: "I have many feelings on this September 18th Memorial Day. The Northeast has been occupied for three years, and although the lost territory has not yet been recovered, the people and the government have never forgotten their determination to recover the lost territory. What I hope for from my compatriots is that at this time when foreign aggression is imminent, we should unite as one and focus on the four words of recovering the lost territory, remember them in our hearts, endure hardship and humiliation, and swear to avenge this humiliation, and then the recovery of the lost territory can be expected in the near future."

(Reasons for Failure: Lack of Contact) According to the written answers of former Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting to reporters: (Question) What are your thoughts on the failure to be elected as a permanent member of the League of Nations? (Answer) We should strive to become stronger. (Question) Will the failure to be elected affect the current political situation in the Far East, and will China be in an unfavorable position? (Answer) Not necessarily. (Question) What is the background and significance of the League of Nations not passing China's re-election? (Answer) Probably due to lack of contact with various countries in peacetime. (Question) Is there a close relationship with the issue of the Soviet Union's joining the League of Nations this time? (Answer) Yes. (Question) Should China seek countermeasures or remain silent? (Answer) Of course, remain silent. It should not be regarded as a major event. When powerful countries such as Germany and Russia join, they can obtain the qualifications of permanent members. I hope the people will pay attention to internal affairs. Only with internal affairs can there be foreign affairs, which is what Guan Zhong meant by "If internal affairs are not cultivated, external affairs will not be successful."

Jiangsu Provincial Government Borrows 200,000 Yuan from Shanghai Banking Community 114

To Purchase Autumn Cocoons to Assist Farmers

Borrowed from China and Jiangsu's Four Agricultural Banks

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, in order to purchase autumn cocoons and assist farmers, the Jiangsu Provincial Government borrowed 200,000 yuan from four banks, including the Bank of China, using the purchased autumn cocoons as collateral. The loan contract will be signed soon. According to details obtained by the Xinsheng News Agency reporter:

(Borrow Money to Purchase Cocoons) After the sharp decline in exports of our country's silk industry, all silk factories were unable to maintain and ceased operations. This year's sharp decline in silk prices is unprecedented. Silk merchants regard the purchase of cocoons as a daunting task. Therefore, this year's autumn cocoons have few consultants. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has borrowed money to collect and reel silk itself. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, considering that the autumn cocoons in Jintan, Liyang, and other places are about to be on the market, but no one is buying them, decided to borrow money from four banks, including China, Jiaotong, Jiangsu, and Farmers, to assist the rural areas, under the direction of Director of Construction Department Shen Baixian.

(Agreed Amount) After Director Shen had initial contact with the town branches of the four banks, including the Bank of China, he came to Shanghai again for consultation. The amount was 200,000 yuan, with all the purchased autumn cocoons as collateral. After the autumn cocoons are sold, the loan will be repaid continuously. The interest rate and contract are still under negotiation. The banks have expressed their agreement that this loan is to assist farmers, so there will be no other problems. Once the contract is negotiated, it can be signed.

(Copies Sent to Each Bank for Signature) After the four identical copies of the contract were transcribed, personnel were immediately dispatched to the fourteen banks to have the general manager sign them. However, due to time constraints, only China, Jiaotong, Zhejiang Industrial, Shanghai Commercial, Zhongnan, Jincheng, Yanye, Dalu, China National Goods, Zhejiang Industrial, China General Commercial, and China Reclamation signed yesterday. The remaining China Industrial and Siming banks will supplement their signatures this morning.

(Zeng Returned to Hangzhou Last Night) Zeng Yangfu believed that the loan issue had been completely handled, so he took the Shanghai-Zhapu express train back to Hangzhou yesterday at 6:50 PM, accompanied by Shou Jingwei, a representative of the Bank of China in Hangzhou. As for the China Industrial Bank and Siming Bank, which had not yet signed, Wang Guohua, Secretary of the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, stayed in Shanghai to handle them. After signing with the two banks this morning, he will take the Shanghai-Hangzhou train back to the province to report back.

Yang Can San Discusses Negotiations in England 117

According to rumors, mineral mortgage loans are completely fictitious.

It is said that they will apply for verification in accordance with Chinese law.

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, Yang Can San, the general manager of Juxingcheng Bank, has attracted attacks from academic circles and attention from society for his investment negotiations in England. A reporter learned of his return to China and went to the bank yesterday to inquire about the truth and his opinions on the matter. The following is a record of the conversation. According to Mr. Yang, this trip abroad to investigate industries was to fulfill a long-cherished wish from ten years ago. It was purely a personal act and had nothing to do with the Sichuan government. The rumor that he was sent by Liu Xiang is absolutely untrue. Liu Xiang has a telegram that can prove this. This should be stated in advance. Currently, there are approximately three major points of attack: (1) Some say that England has long harbored conspiracies in Tibet, and if they invest in Sichuan, it is inevitable that they will have aggressive ambitions. I have also considered this kind of concern, so the first article of the contract clearly stipulates that registration and establishment must be in accordance with Chinese law, in order to prevent it with the power of national law. Moreover, in the past, the contract was made between the government and a foreign country or consortium. The government's position was sufficient to represent the country and the local area, and a slight carelessness could easily lead to invasion. If a private individual in our country engages in commercial activities with a private individual in another country under our country's law, the nature belongs to the scope of civil law and does not affect national sovereignty at all. Therefore, they have no possibility of aggression. Their investment in us, in addition to verifying legitimate uses, does not require any collateral. If the business fails, there are no movable or immovable properties to exercise their right of disposal. Legally speaking, there is really nothing to worry about. Furthermore, based on factual investigations, that country is experiencing economic recession and surplus capital. Deposit interest rates are extremely low, and placement is very difficult. Generally, businessmen are seeking their own ways out to avoid personal economic losses. Their motive is purely to put their own capital in a profitable place and has no political implications. The situations now and in the past are different, and it seems unnecessary to confuse them with overly sensitive nerves. (2) Some say that this approach conflicts with the government's economic control. They do not know that the nature of the government's economic control is active, enabling the people to seek production and construction under the control of the law, rather than preventing the people from doing anything. The financial company is completely subject to Chinese law and does not conflict with the government's control principles. If the government sometimes considers it an obstacle, it can also revise the law at any time to remedy it. In general, the spirit of control should be to ensure that business progresses, production increases, and that control is not lost. (3) Some say that this behavior is to steal all of Sichuan's mineral resources and lose national sovereignty. They do not know that this contract is intended to form a financial company of an introductory nature, preparing for Sichuan's future entrustment of industrial operators to introduce funds. The investment method stipulated is only to indicate that this is the only way to handle it. It is not a loan, so how can there be a mortgage? Even if it is an investment, it is credit. Moreover, it is a private act, and without the government's entrustment, how can it involve all of Sichuan's mineral resources? Anyone with common sense should be able to judge this kind of slander and does not need further explanation. Thinking deeply about saving the country now, empty words are of no help. Production and construction should be the top priority. Sichuan Province has suffered from wars and red disasters. The land of abundance has been impoverished. If we do not follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, and make use of foreign capital to vigorously develop construction, it will not be successful. However, foreign capital is not without its drawbacks. After repeated consideration and discussion with friends, we believe that the following five principles should be prepared: (1) Respect national laws and do not harm national sovereignty; (2) Indirect investment, not direct joint ventures; (3) No collateral; (4) Freedom to borrow and repay loans; (5) No monopoly. Based on the above principles, the financial company formed this time is required to register and establish in accordance with Chinese law (Article 1 of the contract). In the future, the industries to be operated should send exploration teams to investigate, and when foreign capital is needed for development, the permission of the government authorities and the public should be obtained (Article 8 of the contract). The board of directors of the financial company will consist of three Chinese directors, with one as chairman, and two Western directors (Article 5 of the contract). In the event of disputes over the terms, Chinese will prevail (Article 24 of the contract). Furthermore, at any time, if it is discovered that it conflicts with China's national interests, it can be proposed to amend it (Supplementary Article 1). Various provisions emphasize national sovereignty, which is in line with the first principle. The industries that Sichuan intends to operate, that is, the hypothetical cooperative company, will collect considerable funds themselves. The financial company will review the project and, if it is appropriate, agree to provide the funds. Capitalists can only hand over the funds to the financial company and do not directly borrow or invest in the industrial group, adopting indirect principles to avoid interference (Article 3 of the contract). This is in line with the second principle. The industries operated by the cooperative company, in addition to being investigated and researched by the financial company, which is responsible for providing loans and sending accountants to supervise the accounts, do not have any collateral (Article 8 of the contract). This is in line with the third principle. The financial company has no right to interfere with whether or not Sichuan industrial groups use foreign capital. When both parties agree and entrust the company to raise funds on their behalf, Chinese people can invest as much as possible, or when the business is established and benefits are seen, domestic people believe it is safe and are willing to invest. After a considerable period of time, funds can be raised to repay all foreign capital and completely break away from the financial company. This can be said to be a temporary use with clear objectives for both advancing and retreating (Article 15 of the contract), which is in line with the fourth principle. For any business, the most taboo after a country invests is to exclude other countries and have a monopoly. This contract does not limit the funds provided by the company to British nationals. People of any nationality can join (Article 3 of the contract). In addition, the principle is to employ Chinese people and purchase Chinese products. If materials must be borrowed from other places, it is not limited to any nationality (Articles 20 and 21 of the contract). This is in line with the fifth principle. I am not wise or capable enough, and my worries may not be all-encompassing, but I am confident that I have not dared to slack off in the slightest in respecting national sovereignty and building and saving the country. Soon, I will submit the contract in gold to the government for verification. If there are any inappropriate parts, I will respectfully comply with any instructions. I will also sincerely accept any criticisms from all sectors for detailed research on the articles. If it is beneficial to the country, I will not be afraid to seek details and will have no prejudice. If I am slandered with empty and unfounded political arguments, then I dare not listen to them. The reporter asked Mr. Yang when he would return to Sichuan. He replied that since Governor Liu resigned from Sichuan, a financial panic has been triggered in Chongqing. I have repeatedly received telegrams from Chongqing urging me to return to Sichuan in the next few days.
